## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 86 page(s) - 86 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**Issue**: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<p class="usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://medicare.gov/
- https://medicare.gov/about-us/accessibility-nondiscrimination-notice
- https://medicare.gov/basics/forms-publications-mailings/mailings/help-with-costs/copayment-changing
- https://medicare.gov/coverage/find-alphabetically
- https://medicare.gov/coverage/search
- *...and 81 more page(s)*

#### Pattern 2: Affects 74 page(s) - 74 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<button type="button" class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--ghost SimpleFooter__linkButton" data-once="footer-privacy-setting-trigger">Privacy Setting</button>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/button[@class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--ghost SimpleFooter__linkButton"]
```

**How to Replicate**:

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://medicare.gov/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="ch-c-change-language-link ds-u-text-decoration--underline" data-testid="lng-tgl-btn" href="https://es.medicare.gov/" lang="es" data-listener-attached="true">Cambiar a español</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ch-c-change-language-link ds-u-text-decoration--underline"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a data-component-type="card" class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--solid tab-icon-card__cta-link" href="https://www.medicare.gov/plan-compare/" data-listener-attached="true">Find Plans Now</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--solid tab-icon-card__cta-link"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/health-drug-plans" rel="noopener" data-drupal-link-system-path="node/110756" data-listener-attached="true">Health & drug plans</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--ghost SimpleFooter__linkButton" data-once="footer-privacy-setting-trigger">Privacy Setting</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--ghost SimpleFooter__linkButton"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R17](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r17)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<form action="/search/medicare" method="get" id="search-block-form" accept-charset="UTF-8" role="search" class="search-form search-block-form" aria-hidden="true" data-once="searchPII">...</form>`
- XPath: `/form[@id="search-block-form"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.46:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="tab-icon-card__summary">Access your information anytime, anywhere</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="tab-icon-card__summary"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="form-block__intro-text">Get reminders about open enrollment, ways to save ...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="form-block__intro-text"]`

### https://medicare.gov/about-us/accessibility-nondiscrimination-notice

- Message: Target has insufficient size

#### Rule: [SIA-R17](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r17)

- HTML: `<form action="/search/medicare" method="get" id="search-block-form" accept-charset="UTF-8" role="search" class="search-form search-block-form" aria-hidden="true" data-once="searchPII">...</form>`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.46:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`

### https://medicare.gov/basics/forms-publications-mailings/mailings/help-with-costs/copayment-changing

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="ch-c-change-language-link ds-u-text-decoration--underline" data-testid="lng-tgl-btn" href="https://es.medicare.gov/basics/forms-publications-mailings/mailings/help-with-costs/copayment-changing" lang="es">Cambiar a español</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ch-c-change-language-link ds-u-text-decoration--underline"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/" data-listener-attached="true">Home</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--ghost SimpleFooter__linkButton" data-once="footer-privacy-setting-trigger">Privacy Setting</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--ghost SimpleFooter__linkButton"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R17](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r17)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<form action="/search/medicare" method="get" id="search-block-form" accept-charset="UTF-8" role="search" class="search-form search-block-form" aria-hidden="true" data-once="searchPII">...</form>`
- XPath: `/form[@id="search-block-form"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.46:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

### https://medicare.gov/basics/reporting-medicare-fraud-and-abuse

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="ch-c-change-language-link ds-u-text-decoration--underline" data-testid="lng-tgl-btn" href="https://es.medicare.gov/basics/reporting-medicare-fraud-and-abuse" lang="es">Cambiar a español</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ch-c-change-language-link ds-u-text-decoration--underline"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/" data-listener-attached="true">Home</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a data-component-type="dynamic-card-block" class="ds-c-button dynamic-card-block__cta-link ds-c-button--solid ds-c-button--alternate" href="https://www.identitytheft.gov/#/" data-once="dynamic-card-block-cta-link" data-listener-attached="true">Report Identity Theft</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ds-c-button dynamic-card-block__cta-link ds-c-button--solid ds-c-button--alternate"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--ghost SimpleFooter__linkButton" data-once="footer-privacy-setting-trigger">Privacy Setting</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--ghost SimpleFooter__linkButton"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button class="video-embed-field-lazy-play" aria-label="Play video">Play the video YouTube \| Protect Yourself from Enr...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="video-embed-field-lazy-play"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R17](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r17)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<form action="/search/medicare" method="get" id="search-block-form" accept-charset="UTF-8" role="search" class="search-form search-block-form" aria-hidden="true" data-once="searchPII">...</form>`
- XPath: `/form[@id="search-block-form"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.46:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.46:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5

#### Rule: [SIA-R17](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r17)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<form action="/search/medicare" method="get" id="search-block-form" accept-charset="UTF-8" role="search" class="search-form search-block-form" aria-hidden="true" data-once="searchPII">...</form>`
- XPath: `/form[@id="search-block-form"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.46:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5

- XPath: `/form[@id="search-block-form"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.46:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>There are programs run by the states that can help...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>Use the links below to view archived versions of M...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="ch-c-change-language-link ds-u-text-decoration--underline" data-testid="lng-tgl-btn" href="https://es.medicare.gov/health-drug-plans" lang="es">Cambiar a español</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ch-c-change-language-link ds-u-text-decoration--underline"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/" data-listener-attached="true">Home</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a data-component-type="dynamic-card-block" class="ds-c-button dynamic-card-block__cta-link ds-c-button--solid ds-c-button--transparent" href="/health-drug-plans/health-plans" data-listener-attached="true" data-once="dynamic-card-block-cta-link">Understand Health Plans</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ds-c-button dynamic-card-block__cta-link ds-c-button--solid ds-c-button--transparent"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/health-drug-plans" rel="noopener" data-drupal-link-system-path="node/110756" class="is-active" aria-current="page" data-listener-attached="true">Health & drug plans</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="is-active"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--ghost SimpleFooter__linkButton" data-once="footer-privacy-setting-trigger">Privacy Setting</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="ds-c-button ds-c-button--ghost SimpleFooter__linkButton"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R17](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r17)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<form action="/search/medicare" method="get" id="search-block-form" accept-charset="UTF-8" role="search" class="search-form search-block-form" aria-hidden="true" data-once="searchPII">...</form>`
- XPath: `/form[@id="search-block-form"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.46:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="text-align-center">Medicare health plans are generally offered by pri...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="text-align-center"]`

- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>Read and order free Medicare products in a variety...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="text-align-center">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="text-align-center"]`

**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/info-and-relationships) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h2 class="layout__section-title-heading">Popular Publications</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@class="layout__section-title-heading"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is not allowed for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.46:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="ds-text-heading--sm">Step 1 of 3</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ds-text-heading--sm"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="ds-u-color--base ds-u-margin-bottom--1 ds-text-heading--sm">PART A COVERAGE START DATE</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ds-u-color--base ds-u-margin-bottom--1 ds-text-heading--sm"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R80: ASCII art has a text alternative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r80)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="ds-text-heading--sm">Step 1 of 3</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ds-text-heading--sm"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="ds-u-color--base ds-u-margin-bottom--1 ds-text-heading--sm">PART A COVERAGE START DATE</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ds-u-color--base ds-u-margin-bottom--1 ds-text-heading--sm"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.46:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.46:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="usa-banner__header-text"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://medicare.gov/prescription-payment-plan

#### Rule: [color-contrast](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/color-contrast?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.3](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.medicare.gov/privacy-policy" <u="">data privacy policy.</a>`
- XPath: `iframe[height="100%"]`

#### Rule: [frame-title](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/frame-title?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Frames must have an accessible name
- HTML: `<iframe data-src="https://surveys.cms.gov/jfe/form/SV_9LbdFueyKSYZ2nk?Q_CHL=si&amp;Q_CanScreenCapture=1" width="100%" height="100%" frameborder="0" name="survey-iframe-SI_6tbIx8xW9ShoDfU" data-name="embedded-iframe-SI_6tbIx8xW9ShoDfU"></iframe>`
- XPath: `iframe[height="100%"]`

#### Rule: [image-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/image-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="https://surveys.CMS.gov/CP/Graphic.php?IM=IM_eECuJsNTdnd7l66" style="width: 448px; height: 297px;" data-image-state="ready">`
- XPath: `iframe[height="100%"]`

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<main id="content" class="ds-l-col--12 ds-u-padding-x--0 primary-content__content">`
- XPath: `#content`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<nav class="social-links " data-component-id="medicare_evo:footer">`
- XPath: `.social-links`

- HTML: `<a href="https://www.medicare.gov/privacy-policy" <u="">data privacy policy.</a>`

#### Rule: [frame-title](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/frame-title?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Frames must have an accessible name
- HTML: `<iframe data-src="https://surveys.cms.gov/jfe/form/SV_9LbdFueyKSYZ2nk?Q_CHL=si&amp;Q_CanScreenCapture=1" width="100%" height="100%" frameborder="0" name="survey-iframe-SI_6tbIx8xW9ShoDfU" data-name="embedded-iframe-SI_6tbIx8xW9ShoDfU"></iframe>`
- XPath: `iframe[height="100%"]`

#### Rule: [image-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/image-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="https://surveys.CMS.gov/CP/Graphic.php?IM=IM_eECuJsNTdnd7l66" style="width: 448px; height: 297px;" data-image-state="ready">`
- XPath: `iframe[height="100%"]`

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<main id="content" class="ds-l-col--12 ds-u-padding-x--0 primary-content__content">`
- XPath: `#content`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<nav class="social-links " data-component-id="medicare_evo:footer">`
- XPath: `.social-links`
